\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{raymath_8h_source_l00005}00005\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ CONVENTIONS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{raymath_8h_source_l00006}00006\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Matrix\ structure\ is\ defined\ as\ row-\/major\ (memory\ layout)\ but\ parameters\ naming\ AND\ all}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{raymath_8h_source_l00007}00007\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ math\ operations\ performed\ by\ the\ library\ consider\ the\ structure\ as\ it\ was\ column-\/major}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{raymath_8h_source_l00008}00008\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ It\ is\ like\ transposed\ versions\ of\ the\ matrices\ are\ used\ for\ all\ the\ maths}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{raymath_8h_source_l00009}00009\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ It\ benefits\ some\ functions\ making\ them\ cache-\/friendly\ and\ also\ avoids\ matrix}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{raymath_8h_source_l00010}00010\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ transpositions\ sometimes\ required\ by\ OpenGL}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{raymath_8h_source_l00011}00011\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Example:\ In\ memory\ order,\ row0\ is\ [m0\ m4\ m8\ m12]\ but\ in\ semantic\ math\ row0\ is\ [m0\ m1\ m2\ m3]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{raymath_8h_source_l00012}00012\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Functions\ are\ always\ self-\/contained,\ no\ function\ use\ another\ raymath\ function\ inside,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{raymath_8h_source_l00013}00013\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ required\ code\ is\ directly\ re-\/implemented\ inside}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{raymath_8h_source_l00014}00014\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Functions\ input\ parameters\ are\ always\ received\ by\ value\ (2\ unavoidable\ exceptions)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{raymath_8h_source_l00015}00015\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Functions\ use\ always\ a\ "{}result"{}\ variable\ for\ return\ (except\ C++\ operators)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{raymath_8h_source_l00016}00016\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ -\/\ Functions\ are\ always\ defined\ inline}}
